   target.tagName === \"TEXTAREA\" ||\n    66→        target.contentEditable === \"true\"\n    67→      ) {\n    68→        return;\n    69→      }\n    70→\n    71→      if (event.key === \"?\") {\n 78→    return () => window.removeEventListener(\"keydown\", handleKeyDown);\n    79→  }, []);\n    80→\n    81→  // ── Shortcuts list for KeyboardShortcutsDialog ───────────────────────────────\n  .trim()\n    63→    .toLowerCase()\n    64→    .split(\" \")\n    65→    .map((part) => {\n    66→      const tokens = part.split(\"+\");\n    67→      const key = tokens[tokens.length - 1];\n    68→      const modifiers: HotkeyModifiers = {\n    69→        ctrl: tokens.includes(\"ctrl\"),\n    70→        shift: tokens.includes(\"shift\"),\n    71→        alt: tokens.includes(\"alt\"),\n    72→        meta: tokens.includes(\"meta\"),\n    73→      };\n    74→      return { key, modifiers };\n    75→    });\n    76→}\n    77→\n    78→/**\n    79→ * Determine whether a keyboard event matches a single step definition.\n    80→ */\n    81→function matchesStep(\n    82→  event: KeyboardEvent,\n    83→  step: { key: string; modifiers: HotkeyModifiers }\n    84→): boolean {\n    85→  const eventKey = event.key.toLowerCase();\n    86→\n    87→  // Modifier state must match exactly.\n    88→  if (!!event.ctrlKey !== !!step.modifiers.ctrl) return false;\n    89→  if (!!event.shiftKey !== !!step.modifiers.shift) return false;\n    90→  if (!!event.altKey !== !!step.modifiers.alt) return false;\n    91→  if (!!event.metaKey !== !!step.modifiers.meta) return false;\n    92→\n    93→  // Normalise common aliases.\n    94→  const normalisedEventKey =\n    95→    eventKey === \"escape\" ? \"escape\" : eventKey === \" \" ? \"space\" : eventKey;\n    96→  const normalisedStepKey =\n    97→    step.key === \"esc\" ? \"escape\" : step.key === \"space\" ? \"space\" : step.key;\n    98→\n    99→  return normalisedEventKey === normalisedStepKey;\n   100→}\n   101→\n   102→/**\n   103→ * Return true when the currently focused element is a form-like element.\n   104→ */\n   105→function isFormElement(target: EventTarget | null): boolean {\n   106→  if (!(target instanceof HTMLElement)) return false;\n   107→  const tag = target.tagName.toLowerCase();\n   108→  return (\n   109→    tag === \"input\" ||\n   110→    tag === \"textarea\" ||\n   111→    tag === \"select\" ||\n   112→    target.isContentEditable\n   113→  );\n   114→}\n   115→\n   116→// ─── Hook ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   117→\n   118→/**\n   119→ * Register a keyboard shortcut and call `handler` when it fires.\n   120→ *\n   121→ * Supports:\n   122→ * - Simple combos:          \"ctrl+k\", \"shift+?\", \"escape\"\n   123→ * - Sequential key presses: \"g d\", \"g k\" (press G then D within the timeout)\n   124→ *\n   125→ * @param keys    The key combo string (see parseKeys for format).\n   126→ * @param handler Called when the shortcut matches.\n   127→ * @param options Optional configuration.\n   128→ *\n   129→ * @example\n   130→ * ```tsx\n   131→ * useHotkeys(\"ctrl+k\", () => setOpen(true), { preventDefault: true });\n   132→ * useHotkeys(\"g d\",   139→): void {\n   140→  const {\n   141→    enableOnFormTags = false,\n   142→    stopPropagation = false,\n   143→    preventDefault = false,\n   144→    eventType = \"keydown\",\n   145→    sequenceTimeout = 1000,\n   146→  } = options;\n   147→\n   148→  // Keep a stable ref to the latest handler so we don't have to re-register\n   149→  // the event listener whenever the handler closure changes.\n   150→  const handlerRef = useRef<HotkeyHandler>(handler);\n   151→  useEffect(() => {\n   152→    handlerRef.current = handler;\n   153→  }, [handler]);\n   154→\n   155→  // Parse 159→  }, [keys]);\n   160→\n   161→  // Track how far through the sequence the user has progressed.\n   162→  const sequenceIndexRef = useRef(0);\n   163→  const sequenceTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);\n   164→\n   165→  const resetSequence = useCallback(() => {\n   166→    sequenceIndexRef.current = 0;\n   167→    if (sequenceTimerRef.current !== null) {\n   168→      clearTimeout(sequenceTimerRef.current);\n   169→      sequenceTimerRef.current = null;\n   170→    }\n   171→  }, []);\n   172→\n   173→  useEffect(() => {\n   174→    const listener = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {\n   175→      // Skip form elements unless explicitly opted in.\n   176→      if (!enableOnFormTags && isFormElement(event.target)) return;\n   177→\n   178→      const steps = stepsRef.current;\n   179→      const currentStep = steps[sequenceIndexRef.current];\n   180→\n   181→      if (!matchesStep(event, currentStep)) {\n   182→        // The key pressed doesn't match the current step.\n   183→        // Try restarting from step 0 in case it matches the first step.\n   184→        if (sequenceIndexRef.current !== 0) {\n   185→          resetSequence();\n   186→          // Re-check from step 0.\n   187→          if (!matchesStep(event, steps[0])) return;\n   188→          // Matches step 0 — fall through.\n   189→        } else {\n   190→          return;\n   191→        }\n   192→      }\n   193→\n   194→      // Matches the current step.\n   195→      if (stopPropagation) event.stopPropagation();\n   196→\n   197→      const nextIndex = sequenceIndexRef.current + 1;\n   198→\n   199→      if (nextIndex < steps.length) {\n   200→        // More steps remain — advance the sequence index and start the timer.\n   201→        sequenceIndexRef.current = nextIndex;\n   202→\n   203→        if (sequenceTimerRef.current !== null) {\n   204→          clearTimeout(sequenceTimerRef.current);\n   205→        }\n   206→        sequenceTimerRef.current = setTimeout(resetSequence, sequenceTimeout);\n   207→      } else {\n   208→        // All steps matched — fire the handler.\n   209→        if (preventDefault) 266→      while (sequenceStatesRef.current.length < currentBindings.length) {\n   267→        sequenceStatesRef.current.push({ index: 0, timer: null });\n   268→      }\n   269→\n   270→ hotkeys at once.\n   232→ *\n   233→ * Internally attaches a single keydown listener and fans out to the matching\n   234→ * binding, so it is safe to pass a dynamic bindings array without violating\n   235→ * React's Rules of Hooks.\n   236→ *\n   237→ * @param bindings  Array of [keys, handler, options?] tuples.\n   238→ *\n   239→ * @example\n   240→ * ```tsx\n   241→ * useHotkeysMultiple([\n   242→ *   [\"ctrl+k\", () => setOpen(true), { preventDefault: true }],\n   243→ *   [\"escape\",  () => setOpen(false)],\n   244→ * ]);\n   245→ * ```\n   246→ */\n   247→export function useHotkeysMultiple(\n   248→  bindings: Array<[string, HotkeyHandler, UseHotkeysOptions?]>\n   249→): void {\n   250→  // Keep a stable ref so the effect doesn't need to re-register on every render.\n   251→  const bindingsRef = useRef(bindings);\n   252→  useEffect(() => {\n   253→    bindingsRef.current = bindings;\n   254→  });\n   255→\n   256→  // Track per-binding sequence state outside the effect so it persists.\n   257→  const sequenceStatesRef = useRef<\n   258→    Array<{ index: number; timer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null }>\n   259→  >([]);\n   260→\n   261→  useEffect(() => {\n   262→    const listener = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {\n   263→      const currentBindings = bindingsRef.current;\n   264→\n   265→      // Ensure per-binding state array is sized correctly.\n   266→      while (sequenceStatesRef.current.length < currentBindings.length) {\n   267→        sequenceStatesRef.current.push({ index: 0, timer: null });\n   268→      }\n   269→\n   270→      currentBindings.forEach(([keys, handler, opts = {}], bindingIdx) => {\n   271→        const {\n   272→          enableOnFormTags = false,\n   273→          stopPropagation = false,\n   274→          preventDefault = false,\n   275→          sequenceTimeout = 1000,\n   276→        } = opts;\n   277→\n   278→        if (!enableOnFormTags && isFormElement(event.target)) return;\n   279→\n   280→        const steps = parseKeys(keys);\n   281→        const state = sequenceStatesRef.current[bindingIdx];\n   282→        const currentStep = steps[state.index];\n   283→\n   284→        const resetSeq = () => {\n   285→          state.index = 0;\n   286→          if (state.timer !== null) {\n   287→            clearTimeout(state.timer);\n   288→            state.timer = null;\n   289→          }\n   290→        };\n   291→\n   292→        if (!matchesStep(event, currentStep)) {\n   293→          if (state.index !== 0) {\n   294→            resetSeq();\n   295→            if (!matchesStep(event, steps[0])) return;\n   296→          } else {\n   297→            return;\n   298→          }\n   299→        }\n   300→\n   301→        if (stopPropagation) event.stopPropagation();\n   302→\n   303→        const nextIndex = state.index + 1;\n   304→        if (nextIndex < steps.length) {\n   305→          state.index = nextIndex;\n   306→          if (state.timer !== null) clearTimeout(state.timer);\n   307→          state.timer = setTimeout(resetSeq, sequenceTimeout);\n   308→        } else {\n   309→          if (preventDefault) event.preventDefault();\n   310→          resetSeq();\n   311→          handler(event);\n   312→        }\n   313→      });\n   314→    };\n   315→\n   316→    window.addEventListener(\"keydown\", listener);\n   317→    return () => {\n   318→      window.removeEventListener(\"keydown\", listener);\n   319→      // Clear any pending timers.\n   320→      sequenceStatesRef.current.forEach((state) => {\n   321→        if (state.timer !== null) clearTimeout(state.timer);\n   322→      });\n   323→      sequenceStatesRef.current = [];\n   324→    };\n   325→  // Re-register only when the number of bindings changes (keys/options checked\n   326→  // via the ref inside the listener).\n   327→  }, [bindings.length]);\n   328→}\n   329→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be Fan-out pattern for efficient event handling\n\n### 3. **High-Level Hook** (`src/hooks/use-keyboard-shortcuts.ts`)\n- **useKeyboardShortcuts()**: Orchestrates all app-wide shortcuts\n  - Navigation sequences via useHotkeys (G+D, G+K, G+S, G+A, G+G)\n  - structured representation.\n    55→ *\n    56→ * Sequential combos are separated by a single space, e.g. \"g d\".\n    57→ * Within each step, modifiers and the key are joined by \"+\".\n    58→ */\n    59→function parseKeys(keys: string): Array<{ key: string; modifiers: HotkeyModifiers }> {\n    60→  // Each space-separated part is one step in a potential sequence.\n    61→  return keys\n    62→    .trim()\n    63→    .toLowerCase()\n    64→    .split(\" \")\n    65→    .map((part) => {\n    66→      const tokens = part.split(\"+\");\n    67→      const key = tokens[tokens.length - 1];\n    68→      const modifiers: HotkeyModifiers = {\n    69→        ctrl: tokens.includes(\"ctrl\"),\n    70→        shift: tokens.includes(\"shift\"),\n    71→        alt: tokens.includes(\"alt\"),\n    72→        meta: tokens.includes(\"meta\"),\n    73→      };\n    74→      return { key, modifiers };\n    75→    });\n    76→}\n    77→\n    78→/**\n    79→ * Determine whether a keyboard event matches a single step definition.\n    80→ */\n    81→function matchesStep(\n    82→  event: KeyboardEvent,\n    83→  step: { key: string; modifiers: HotkeyModifiers }\n    84→): boolean {\n    85→  const eventKey = event.key.toLowerCase();\n    86→\n    87→  // Modifier state must match exactly.\n    88→  if (!!event.ctrlKey !== !!step.modifiers.ctrl) return false;\n    89→  if (!!event.shiftKey !== sequenceIndexRef.current = nextIndex;\n   202→\n   203→        if (sequenceTimerRef.current !== null) {\n   204→          clearTimeout(sequenceTimerRef.current);\n   205→        }\n   206→ {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"tooluse_QLE7XZezJ9faRTiFyschM1","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→/**\n     2→ * Custom keybindings persistence layer for KeyVault.\n     3→ *\n     4→ * Stores user-overridden key bindings in localStorage so that customisations\n     5→ * survive page reloads without requiring a backend.\n     6→ *\n     7→ * All localStorage access is guarded with `typeof window !== \"undefined\"` so\n     8→ * this module is safe to import in Next.js SSR contexts.\n     9→ */\n    10→\n    11→import {\n    12→  KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS,\n    13→  ShortcutDefinition,\n    14→} from \"@/lib/keyboard-shortcuts\";\n    15→\n    16→// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    17→\n    18→/**\n    19→ * A single user-defined override for one of the built-in shortcuts.\n    20→ */\n    21→export interface CustomBinding {\n    22→  /** The id of the ShortcutDefinition being overridden. */\n    23→  shortcutId: string;\n    24→  /**\n    25→   * The custom key combo string in the same format used by useHotkeys,\n    26→   * e.g. \"ctrl+shift+k\" or \"g d\".\n    27→   */\n    28→  keys: string;\n    29→  /** Display-friendly label, e.g. \"Ctrl+Shift+K\" or \"G then D\". */\n    30→  keysLabel: string;\n    31→}\n    32→\n    33→// ─── Constants ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    34→\n    35→export const STORAGE_KEY = \"keyvault-custom-keybindings\";\n    36→\n    37→// ─── Storage helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    38→\n    39→/**\n    40→ * Read all custom bindings from localStorage.\n    41→ * Returns an empty array if localStorage is unavailable or the stored value\n    42→ * is invalid / corrupt.\n    43→ */\n    44→export function getCustomBindings(): CustomBinding[] {\n    45→  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return [];\n    46→\n    47→  try {\n    48→    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);\n    49→    if (!raw) return [];\n    50→    const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);\n    51→    if (!Array.isArray(parsed)) return [];\n    52→    // Basic shape validation — filter out any malformed entries.\n    53→    return parsed.filter(\n    54→      (item): item is CustomBinding =>\n    55→        typeof item === \"object\" &&\n    56→        item !== null &&\n    57→        typeof item.shortcutId === \"string\" &&\n    58→        typeof item.keys === \"string\" &&\n    59→        typeof item.keysLabel === \"string\"\n    60→    );\n    61→  } catch {\n    62→    return [];\n    63→  }\n    64→}\n    65→\n    66→/**\n    67→ * Persist the given bindings array to localStorage.\n    68→ * Silently swallows errors (e.g. private browsing with storage blocked).\n    69→ */\n    70→function saveCustomBindings(bindings: CustomBinding[]): void {\n    71→  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return;\n    72→  try {\n    73→    window.localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(bindings));\n    74→  } catch {\n    75→    // localStorage quota exceeded or blocked — nothing we can do.\n    76→  }\n    77→}\n    78→\n    79→// ─── CRUD operations ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n    80→\n    81→/**\n    82→ * Upsert a custom binding for the given shortcut.\n    83→ * If a binding already exists for `shortcutId` it will be replaced.\n    84→ */\n    85→export function setCustomBinding(\n    86→  shortcutId: string,\n    87→  keys: string,\n    88→  keysLabel: string\n    89→): void {\n    90→  const existing = getCustomBindings().filter(\n    91→    (b) => b.shortcutId !== shortcutId\n    92→  );\n    93→  saveCustomBindings([...existing, { shortcutId, keys, keysLabel }]);\n    94→}\n    95→\n    96→/**\n    97→ * Remove any custom binding for the given shortcut, reverting it to its\n    98→ * default.\n    99→ */\n   100→export function removeCustomBinding(shortcutId: string): void {\n   101→  saveCustomBindings(\n   102→    getCustomBindings().filter((b) => b.shortcutId !== shortcutId)\n   103→  );\n   104→}\n   105→\n   106→/**\n   107→ * Clear all custom bindings, reverting every shortcut to its default.\n   108→ */\n   109→export function resetAllBindings(): void {\n   110→  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return;\n   111→  try {\n   112→    window.localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);\n   113→  } catch {\n   114→    // Swallow errors.\n   115→  }\n   116→}\n   117→\n   118→// ─── Derived / lookup helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   119→\n   120→/**\n   121→ * Return `true` when the user has a custom binding stored for `shortcutId`.\n   122→ */\n   123→export function hasCustomBinding(shortcutId: string): boolean {\n   124→  return getCustomBindings().some((b) => b.shortcutId === shortcutId);\n   125→}\n   126→\n   127→/**\n   128→ * Return the effective ShortcutDefinition for a given id.\n   129→ *\n   130→ * If the user has a custom binding for this shortcut the `keys` and\n   131→ * `keysLabel` fields will reflect that override; all other fields\n   132→ * (id, label, description, category) remain unchanged.\n   133→ *\n   134→ * @throws {Error} When `shortcutId` does not exist in KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.\n   135→ */\n   136→export function getEffectiveShortcut(shortcutId: string): ShortcutDefinition {\n   137→  const base = KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.find((s) => s.id === shortcutId);\n   138→  if (!base) {\n   139→    throw new Error(\n   140→      `[custom-keybindings] Unknown shortcut id: \"${shortcutId}\"`\n   141→    );\n   142→  }\n   143→\n   144→  const custom = getCustomBindings().find((b) => b.shortcutId === shortcutId);\n   145→  if (!custom) return base;\n   146→\n   147→  return { ...base, keys: custom.keys, keysLabel: custom.keysLabel };\n   148→}\n   149→\n   150→/**\n   151→ * Return all shortcuts with any user overrides applied.\n   152→ * Preserves the original order of KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.\n   153→ */\n   154→export function getEffectiveShortcuts(): ShortcutDefinition[] {\n   155→  const customs = getCustomBindings();\n   156→  const customMap = new Map(customs.map((c) => [c.shortcutId, c]));\n   157→\n   158→  return KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.map((shortcut) => {\n   159→    const custom = customMap.get(shortcut.id);\n   160→    if (!custom) return shortcut;\n   161→    return { ...shortcut, keys: custom.keys, keysLabel: custom.keysLabel };\n   162→  });\n   163→}\n   164→\n   165→/**\n   166→ * Given a proposed key combo for `shortcutId`, return any OTHER shortcuts\n   167→ * that already use the same `keys` string (either via a custom binding or\n   168→ * their default).  An empty array means no conflict.\n   169→ */\n   170→export function detectConflicts(\n   171→  shortcutId: string,\n   172→  keys: string\n   173→): ShortcutDefinition[] {\n   174→  const normalised = keys.trim().toLowerCase();\n   175→  return getEffectiveShortcuts().filter(\n   176→    (s) => s.id !== shortcutId && s.keys.trim().toLowerCase() === normalised\n   177→  );\n   178→}\n   179→\n   180→// ─── Formatting helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n   181→\n   182→/**\n   183→ * Convert a raw keys string into a human-readable display label.\n   184→ *\n   185→ * Rules:\n   186→ * - ShortcutDefinition,\n} from \"@/lib/keyboard-shortcuts\";\n\n// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/**\n * A single user-defined override for one of the built-in shortcuts.\n */\nexport interface CustomBinding {\n  /** The id of the ShortcutDefinition being overridden. */\n  shortcutId: string;\n  /**\n   * The custom key combo string in the same format used by useHotkeys,\n   * e.g. \"ctrl+shift+k\" or \"g d\".\n   */\n  keys: string;\n  /** Display-friendly label, e.g. \"Ctrl+Shift+K\" or \"G then D\". */\n  keysLabel: string;\n}\n\n// ─── Constants ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nexport const STORAGE_KEY = \"keyvault-custom-keybindings\";\n\n// ─── Storage helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/**\n * Read all custom bindings from localStorage.\n * Returns an empty array if localStorage is unavailable or the stored value\n * is &&\n        typeof item.keys === \"string\" &&\n        typeof item.keysLabel === \"string\"\n    );\n  } catch {\n    return [];\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Persist the given bindings array to localStorage.\n * Silently swallows errors (e.g. private browsing with storage blocked).\n */\nfunction saveCustomBindings(bindings: CustomBinding[]): void {\n  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return;\n  try {\n removeCustomBinding(shortcutId: string): void {\n  saveCustomBindings(\n    getCustomBindings().filter((b) => b.shortcutId !== shortcutId)\n  );\n}\n\n/**\n * Clear all custom bindings, reverting every shortcut to its default.\n */\nexport function resetAllBindings(): void {\n  if (typeof window === \"undefined\") return;\n  try {\n    window.localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);\n  } catch {\n    // Swallow errors.\n  }\n}\n\n// ─── Derived / lookup helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/**\n * Return `true` when the user has a custom binding stored for `shortcutId`.\n */\nexport function hasCustomBinding(shortcutId: string): boolean {\n  return getCustomBindings().some((b) => b.shortcutId === shortcutId);\n}\n\n/**\n * Return the effective ShortcutDefinition for a given id.\n *\n * If the user has a custom binding for this shortcut the `keys` and\n * `keysLabel` fields will reflect that override; all other fields\n * (id, label, description, category) remain unchanged.\n *\n * @throws {Error} When `shortcutId` does not exist in KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.\n */\nexport function getEffectiveShortcut(shortcutId: string): ShortcutDefinition {\n  const base = KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.find((s) => s.id === shortcutId);\n  if (!base) {\n    throw new Error(\n      `[custom-keybindings] Unknown shortcut id: \"${shortcutId}\"`\n    );\n  }\n\n  const custom = getCustomBindings().find((b) => b.shortcutId === shortcutId);\n  if (!custom) return base;\n\n  return { ...base, keys: custom.keys, keysLabel: custom.keysLabel };\n}\n\n/**\n * Return all shortcuts with any user overrides applied.\n * Preserves the original order of KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.\n */\nexport function getEffectiveShortcuts(): ShortcutDefinition[] {\n  const customs = getCustomBindings();\n  const customMap = new Map(customs.map((c) => [c.shortcutId, c]));\n\n  return KEYBOARD_SHORTCUTS.map((shortcut) => {\n    const custom = customMap.get(shortcut.id);\n    if (!custom) return shortcut;\n    return { ...shortcut, keys: custom.keys, keysLabel: custom.keysLabel };\n  });\n}\n\n/**\n * Given a proposed key combo for `shortcutId`, return any OTHER shortcuts\n * that already use the same `keys` string (either via a custom binding or\n * their default).  An empty array means no conflict.\n */\nexport function detectConflicts(\n  shortcutId: string,\n  keys: string\n): ShortcutDefinition[] {\n  const normalised = keys.trim().toLowerCase();\n  return getEffectiveShortcuts().filter(\n    (s) => s.id !== shortcutId && s.keys.trim().toLowerCase() === normalised\n  );\n}\n\n// ─── Formatting helper ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/**\n * Convert a raw keys string into a human-readable display label.\n *\n * Rules:\n * - Sequential keys (space-separated, no modifier on any step) → \"X then Y\"\n * - Modifier combos (joined by \"+\") → capitalise each token and rejoin with \"+\"\n * - Mixed / edge cases fall back to a best-effort capitalisation.\n *\n * Examples:\n *   \"ctrl+shift+k\" → \"Ctrl+Shift+K\"\n *   \"g d\"          → \"G then D\"\n *   \"escape\"       → \"Escape\"\n *   \"?\"            → \"?\"\n */\nexport function formatKeysLabel(keys: string): string {\n  const trimmed = keys.trim().toLowerCase();\n\n  // Split on spaces to detect multi-step sequences.\n  const parts = trimmed.split(\" \").filter(Boolean);\n\n  // Capitalise a single token, e.g. \"ctrl\" → \"Ctrl\", \"k\" → \"K\".\n  const capitalise = (token: string): string =>\n    token.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + token.slice(1);\n\n  // A single step that contains \"+\" is a modifier combo.\n  const formatStep = (step: string): string =>\n    step\n      .split(\"+\")\n      .map(capitalise)\n      .join(\"+\");\n\n  if (parts.length === 1) {\n    // Single step, e.g. \"ctrl+k\" or \"escape\" or \"?\".\n    return formatStep(parts[0]);\n  }\n\n  // Multiple parts — check whether ALL parts are single characters (no \"+\"),\n  // which indicates a sequential combo like \"g d\".\n  const allSingleKey = parts.every((p) => !p.includes(\"+\"));\n  if (allSingleKey) {\n    return parts.map((p) => p.toUpperCase()).join(\" then \");\n  }\n\n  // Mixed / unexpected format — capitalise each step joined by a space.\n  return parts.map(formatStep).join(\" \");\n}\n","numLines":228,"startLine":1,"totalLines":228}}}
